msg:This Hyatt may be a drag on the overall Hyatt. And compared to the Hyatt in Lijiang where I just stayed, Wuhan Hyatt may only have 75 points.
Let's talk about the front desk first. The design is weird. The check-in waiter stands shorter than the customer. The customer sees the waiter's workbench completely. It looks very messy if there are a few more documents. Then I booked 4 nights in two orders with the same name. The waiter couldn't find it even with my ID card. She woke up from the dream when I told her that there were four nights in total. It was not until the next day that I was told that the room type I booked was different. Either add 300 or move. After staying for one night, I found that it was not very good, so I decided to cancel the next two nights and go to Marriott.
The room is relatively large, 50 square meters. But the bed is surprisingly small. People like us who are short think the bed is small. I sleep with my child, so I have to put the bed together for comfort. The bed should not be more than 1.1 meters wide. The bed is not as big as it looks in the photo. If you are like me with my second child, you can ask about the width of the bed first.
The floor of the shower room is very smooth, like skating. Be very careful. Especially for children and the elderly. The water level is very hidden, you can't uncover it yourself, and the water is not smooth, like a small pond. You need to find the engineering depar**ent.
The room attendant is very enthusiastic, which is a plus.
The big brother at the door asked him if he could help call a taxi, and he said, you can go down and call a taxi yourself. We dragged two young children and three elderly people. It was like we were not guests.
Breakfast, it can be considered normal.
If it's 600 yuan, I think this service is normal, but 1100, the service needs to be improved. And it feels that the procurement is watered, especially the bench in the bathroom, which is not filled enough and hurts the butt.

General comment
